Translation Instructions for СRadmast.txtТ


СRadmast.txtТ is a pure text file (NOT MSDos Text).

It contains all of the 'chatter' across the radio that's spoken during the Battle of Britain simulation. We will simultaneously be printing it on the screen.

It's VERY important to note that: Only text within quotes requires translation.

Many of the sentences spoken are made up from words or phrases in different parts of the document.  At the end of every line with text for translation there is an example of how the text will be used.  That example follows the СEg: С, if the text is conte
xt sensitive.

We KNOW that in some languages the ordering of the phrases in the sentence will be different to English.  Where possible try and keep the same ordering.  However, if there are grammatical ordering problems with compound sentences, copy the example we have
 given and paste it on the next line, indicating the ordering change.

The line lengths in the document can be very long and suffer from Сwrap-roundТ when loaded into Word. WordPad does not suffer from this problem.

The edited file must be saved out as a pure Text File.

NOTE - this text has ALREADY been translated into GERMAN by CREA DESIGN so do NOT repeat this process in GERMAN!!
